################################
################################
########## BLACKLOCKS ##########
################################
################################
			
### In order: 	
#
# Line of Thrár
# Line of Zirak ~ vassals in Mablad-dum, survive as unlanded nobles in Barazimabul after the eruption
# Line of Kreyir ~ Axes of Nargubraz who settled in Barazimabul
# Line of Gorovôd ~ Gorovôd the Goblinslayer
# Line of Balauryut ~ counselors of Nargubraz that branched off Thrár's line
# Line of Baruk Odlig ~ 'Axes of the Exiles', the line of Rôn the Exile, first Lord of the Axes of Nargubraz
# Line of Argan	# The axe that walks
# Line of Brúni ~ Blackflame
# Line of Tharân ~ tributaries of Mablad-dum and establishers of the mining colony in Barazimabul
# Line of Ramdin ~ holders of the Barazimabul mining colony after the line of Tharân dies out
# Line of Varâkh ~ vassals in Mablad-dum, earlier nobles of Nargubraz, survive as nobles in Barazimabul after the eruption
# Line of Ozrên ~ surface vassals in Mablad-dum, die out during the volcanic eruption
# Line of Bhalrîm ~ vassals in Mablad-dum, most die out in the eruption, some members survive for a time after fleeing to Luzna-dum, but they die out after the colony in Luzna-dum is overrun
# Line of Ôldur ~ vassals in Mablad-dum, die out in the eruption
# Line of Delir ~ vassals in Mablad-dum, die out in the eruption
# Line of Misrak ~ vassals in Mablad-dum, die out in the eruption
# Line of Dhrâl ~ surface vassals in Mablad-dum, die out in the eruption
# Line of Dhurâm ~ surface vassals in Mablad-dum, survive as unlanded nobles in Barazimabul for a time but die out eventually warring against the Orcs and Goblins
# Line of Thanûl ~ vassals in Mablad-dum, survive as unlanded nobles in Barazimabul after the eruption
# Line of Bohûr ~ vassals in Mablad-dum, survive as unlanded nobles in Barazimabul after the eruption
# Line of Oran ~ vassals in Mablad-dum, Tried to begin an expansion into the west a few generations before the eruption, were Vassals of the Varâkh Dynasty but died off in attacks from the Orcs & Goblins)
# Line of Khodûl ~ founders of the Luzna-dum mining colony, leading to the Blacklocks of Bizaruldum becoming intrigued by the Yellow Mountains, which later lead to the founding of Mablad-dum


##########################
### The Line of Thrár ####
##########################

lineofthrarI = { # Thrár I the Proud, born and died in the years of the Trees
    name = Thr_ar

    dynasty = dynasty_thrar
    religion = faith_eastern_khazad
    culture = blacklocks

    dna = thrar_dna
	
    sexuality = heterosexual

    trait = arrogant
    trait = stubborn
    trait = brave

    # Base stats assigned through lotr_posthistory_effects because character dies during Years of the Trees
	diplomacy = 0
	martial = 0
	stewardship = 0 
	intrigue = 0
	learning = 0
	prowess = 0

	trait = dwarf_father

    diplomacy = 5
    martial = 3
    stewardship = 10
    intrigue = 4
    learning = 5
    prowess = 13

	trait = education_stewardship_5

    2.1.15 = {
        birth = yes
        give_nickname = nick_the_proud_dwarf
        effect = {
            add_character_flag = {
                flag = had_nickname_event
            }
        }
    }

    2.3.15 = {
        add_spouse = lineofthrarIwife
    }


    2.4.18 = {
        death = { death_reason = death_natural_causes }
    }
}
